<p>The <b>2016 AFC Futsal Championship qualification</b> was a men's <a href="/wiki/Futsal" title="Futsal">futsal</a> competition which decided the participating teams of the <a href="/wiki/2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2016 AFC Futsal Championship">2016 AFC Futsal Championship</a>. A total of 16 teams qualified to play in the final tournament, including <a href="/wiki/Japan_national_futsal_team" title="Japan national futsal team">Japan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iran_national_futsal_team" title="Iran national futsal team">Iran</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan_national_futsal_team" title="Uzbekistan national futsal team">Uzbekistan</a> (hosts), who qualified directly as the top three finishers of the <a href="/wiki/2014_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2014 AFC Futsal Championship">2014 AFC Futsal Championship</a>. Since third-placed Uzbekistan qualified automatically as hosts, <a href="/wiki/Kuwait_national_futsal_team" title="Kuwait national futsal team">Kuwait</a>, who finished fourth, would have also qualified as the next best-ranked team,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stage_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-stage-5">[5]</a></sup> but they were later replaced due to FIFA's suspension of the <a href="/wiki/Kuwait_Football_Association" title="Kuwait Football Association">Kuwait Football Association</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-kuwait_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-kuwait-6">[6]</a></sup></p>
<p>The top five teams of the final tournament qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2016_FIFA_Futsal_World_Cup" title="2016 FIFA Futsal World Cup">2016 FIFA Futsal World Cup</a> in Colombia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-distribution_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-distribution-7">[7]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Teams">Teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A total of 26 <a href="/wiki/Asian_Football_Confederation" title="Asian Football Confederation">AFC</a> member national teams entered the qualifying stage, split into zones according to their regional affiliations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-stage_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-stage-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-draw_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-draw-8">[8]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/West_Asian_Football_Federation" title="West Asian Football Federation">West Asia</a> had seven entrants, where they were drawn into one group of four teams and one group of three teams.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Central_Asian_Football_Association" title="Central Asian Football Association">Central Asia</a> had four entrants, where they were all placed in one group.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Asian_Football_Federation" title="South Asian Football Federation">South Asia</a> had no entrants.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/ASEAN_Football_Federation" title="ASEAN Football Federation">ASEAN</a> had ten entrants, with the <a href="/wiki/2015_AFF_Futsal_Championship" title="2015 AFF Futsal Championship">2015 AFF Futsal Championship</a> doubling as the ASEAN qualifiers, where they were drawn into two groups of five teams.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/East_Asian_Football_Federation" title="East Asian Football Federation">East Asia</a> had five entrants, where they were all placed in one group.</li>
</ul>
<p>The draw for the qualifiers was held on 2 September 2015 at the AFC House in <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-draw_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-draw-8">[8]</a></sup> Only the groups in West Asia were drawn, as no draw was necessary for Central Asia and East Asia, and the draw for the 2015 AFF Futsal Championship had already been held on 16 June 2015 in <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></p>
<p>Apart from the four direct qualifiers, the remaining twelve slots in the final tournament were allocated as follows:</p>
<ul>
<li>Each zone (except South Asia) was allocated a minimum of two slots.</li>
<li>Additional slots were allocated based on the technical standard team ranking from fourth to seventh placing in the <a href="/wiki/2014_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2014 AFC Futsal Championship">2014 AFC Futsal Championship</a>, with West Asia (4th and 7th) and ASEAN (5th and 6th) each allocated two additional slots.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-draw_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-draw-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
</ul>

<tr>
<th></th>
<th>Slots +<br/>
Direct qualifiers</th>
<th>Teams entering qualification</th>
<th>Did not enter</th>
</tr>
<tr>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In each group, teams played each other once at a centralised venue. The top two teams of each group (total 12 teams) qualified for the final tournament.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tiebreakers">Tiebreakers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Tiebreakers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The teams were ranked according to <a href="/wiki/Three_points_for_a_win" title="Three points for a win">points</a> (3 points for a win, 1 point for a draw, 0 points for a loss). If tied on points, tiebreakers would be applied in the following order:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-12">[12]</a></sup></p>
<ol>
<li>Greater number of points obtained in the group matches between the teams concerned;</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goal_difference" title="Goal difference">Goal difference</a> resulting from the group matches between the teams concerned;</li>
<li>Greater number of goals scored in the group matches between the teams concerned;</li>
<li>If, after applying criteria 1 to 3, teams still have an equal ranking, criteria 1 to 3 are reapplied exclusively to the matches between the teams in question to determine their final rankings. If this procedure does not lead to a decision, criteria 5 to 9 apply;</li>
<li>Goal difference in all the group matches;</li>
<li>Greater number of goals scored in all the group matches;</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">Penalty shoot-out</a> if only two teams are involved and they are both on the field of play;</li>
<li>Fewer score calculated according to the number of yellow and red cards received in the group matches (1 point for a single yellow card, 3 points for a red card as a consequence of two yellow cards, 3 points for a direct red card, 4 points for a yellow card followed by a direct red card);</li>
<li>Drawing of lots.</li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Zones">Zones</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Zones">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The matches were played on the following dates:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li>West Zone: 1–3 October 2015</li>
<li>ASEAN Zone: 8–16 October 2015</li>
<li>Central Zone: 14–16 November 2015</li>
<li>East Zone: 14–19 November 2015</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="West_Zone">West Zone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: West Zone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>For the draw, the teams were seeded according to their performance in the previous season in 2014.
<ul>
<li>Pot 1: Iraq, Lebanon</li>
<li>Pot 2: Qatar, Saudi Arabia</li>
<li>Pot 3: Bahrain, United Arab Emirates</li>
<li>Pot 4: Jordan</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>All matches were held in <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>.</li>
<li>Times listed were <a href="/wiki/UTC%2B08:00" title="UTC+08:00">UTC+8</a>.</li>
</ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="ASEAN_Zone">ASEAN Zone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_Futsal_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: ASEAN Zone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2015_AFF_Futsal_Championship" title="2015 AFF Futsal Championship">2015 AFF Futsal Championship</a></div>
<ul>
<li>All matches were held in <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>. The tournament was originally to be held in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> before the suspension of its football association.</li>
<li>Times listed were <a href="/wiki/UTC%2B07:00" title="UTC+07:00">UTC+7</a>.</li>
</ul>

<td><span class="sortkey" style="display:none;">10 !</span><span class="sorttext">10</span> (<a href="/wiki/2001_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2001 AFC Futsal Championship">2001</a>, <a href="/wiki/2002_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2002 AFC Futsal Championship">2002</a>, <a href="/wiki/2003_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2003 AFC Futsal Championship">2003</a>, <a href="/wiki/2004_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2004 AFC Futsal Championship">2004</a>, <a href="/wiki/2005_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2005 AFC Futsal Championship">2005</a>, <a href="/wiki/2006_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2006 AFC Futsal Championship">2006</a>, <a href="/wiki/2008_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2008 AFC Futsal Championship">2008</a>, <a href="/wiki/2010_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2010 AFC Futsal Championship">2010</a>, <a href="/wiki/2012_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2012 AFC Futsal Championship">2012</a>, <a href="/wiki/2014_AFC_Futsal_Championship" title="2014 AFC Futsal Championship">2014</a>)</td>
